# Architecture Document: Istio Pilot Discovery Service

**Repository:** istio/istio
**Output:** Write your document to `/workspace/documentation.md`

## Task

Produce an architecture document for **Istio Pilot's Discovery Service** subsystem. The document must explain how Pilot serves xDS (Envoy Discovery Service) configuration to proxies, translates Istio's high-level configuration into Envoy-specific resources, integrates with service registries, and supports multi-cluster deployments. Do not simply list APIs — explain the **design**, **data flow**, and **extension points**.

## Scope

Your document must cover these four components and how they work together:

### 1. DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server
The central component implementing Pilot's gRPC interface for Envoy's xDS APIs. Explain:
- How it implements Envoy's xDS v3 protocol (ADS, incremental/state-of-the-world modes)
- The role of `adsClients` in tracking active proxy connections
- How configuration pushes are coordinated: debouncing, rate limiting, concurrent push limits
- Cache management for xDS resources (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS)
- The lifecycle: initialization, handling new connections, shutdown

### 2. ADS and the Connection Model
The Aggregated Discovery Service stream handler. Explain:
- How `Stream()` establishes a bidirectional gRPC stream with an Envoy proxy
- The `Connection` type: wrapping the stream with proxy metadata and state
- Request processing: how `processRequest()` determines what configuration to send
- Push coordination: how `pushConnection()` transmits updates to a single proxy
- The `StartPush()` broadcast mechanism for fleet-wide updates

### 3. PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation
The immutable configuration snapshot used during a push. Explain:
- What `PushContext` holds: services, destination rules, virtual services, sidecars, gateways
- How `InitContext()` rebuilds the push context when Istio config changes (CRD watches)
- Config translation: how Pilot converts Istio's `VirtualService` and `DestinationRule` into Envoy's `RouteConfiguration` and `Cluster` resources
- The relationship between push triggers (config changes, service registry updates) and push context regeneration
- Metrics and error tracking during push generation

### 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support
The service discovery layer feeding the DiscoveryServer. Explain:
- How `ServiceRegistry` (Kubernetes controller) watches K8s Services, Endpoints, and Pods
- The aggregate controller pattern for multi-registry support (K8s services + `ServiceEntry` resources)
- Multi-cluster support: how Pilot aggregates services from multiple clusters
- How endpoint updates (pod scale-up, health changes) trigger EDS pushes
- The relationship between the service registry and xDS: when does a service change trigger CDS vs. EDS?

## Document Requirements

1. **Component Responsibilities** — what each component owns
2. **Data Flow** — the path from Istio config change → DiscoveryServer → xDS push to Envoy proxies
3. **Extension Points** — where users extend Istio (custom config translation, external service registries, telemetry plugins)
4. **Error Handling** — how errors at each stage (config validation, push failures, proxy disconnects) are handled
5. **relevant source files** — reference the actual source files in the istio/istio repository (e.g., `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`)

## Anti-Requirements

- Do NOT generate a simple API listing or struct dump
- Do NOT fabricate type names or file paths that don't exist in the repository
- Do NOT cover Istio components outside the Pilot discovery path (e.g., Citadel, Galley, sidecar injection)

   356→// PushRequest defines a request to push to proxies
   357→// It is used to send updates to the config update debouncer and pass to the PushQueue.
   358→type PushRequest struct {
   359→	// Full determines whether a full push is required or not. If false, an incremental update will be sent.
   360→	// Incremental pushes:
   361→	// * Do not recompute the push context
   362→	// * Do not recompute proxy state (such as ServiceInstances)
   363→	// * Are not reported in standard metrics such as push time
   364→	// As a result, configuration updates should never be incremental. Generally, only EDS will set this, but
   365→	// in the future SDS will as well.
   366→	Full bool
   367→
   368→	// ConfigsUpdated keeps track of configs that have changed.
   369→	// This is used as an optimization to avoid unnecessary pushes to proxies that are scoped with a Sidecar.
   370→	// If this is empty, then all proxies will get an update.
   371→	// Otherwise only proxies depend on these configs will get an update.
   372→	// The kind of resources are defined in pkg/config/schemas.
   373→	ConfigsUpdated sets.Set[ConfigKey]
   374→
   375→	AddressesUpdated sets.Set[string]
   376→
   377→	// Push stores the push context to use for the update. This may initially be nil, as we will
   378→	// debounce changes before a PushContext is eventually created.
   379→	Push *PushContext
   380→
   381→	// Start represents the time a push was started. This represents the time of adding to the PushQueue.
   382→	// Note that this does not include time spent debouncing.
   383→	Start time.Time
   384→
   385
... (truncated)

   150→		wis, r := p.AddressInformation(addresses)
   151→		if len(wis) == 0 && len(r) == 0 {
   152→			continue
   153→		}
   154→		foundRegistryCount++
   155→		if foundRegistryCount == 1 {
   156→			// first registry: use the data structures they provided, to avoid a copy
   157→			removed = r
   158→			i = wis
   159→		} else {
   160→			i = append(i, wis...)
   161→			removed.Merge(r)
   162→		}
   163→	}
   164→	if foundRegistryCount > 1 {
   165→		// We may have 'removed' it in one registry but found it in another
   166→		// As an optimization, we skip this in the common case of only one registry
   167→		for _, wl := range i {
   168→			// TODO(@hzxuzhonghu) This is not right for workload, we may search workload by ip, but the resource name is uid.
   169→			if removed.Contains(wl.ResourceName()) {
   170→				removed.Delete(wl.ResourceName())
   171→			}
   172→		}
   173→	}
   174→	return i, removed
   175→}
   176→
   177→func (c *Controller) ServiceInfo(key string) *model.ServiceInfo {
   178→	if !features.EnableAmbientMultiNetwork {
   179→		return nil
   180→	}
   181→	for _, p := range c.GetRegistries() {
   182→		// When it comes to service info in ambient multicluster setup, only the local cluster matter.
   183→		if p.Cluster() == c.configClusterID && p.Provider() == provider.Kubernetes {
   184→			return p.ServiceInfo(key)
   185→		}
   186→	}
   187→	return nil
   188→}
   189→
   190→type registryEntry struct {
   191→	serviceregistry.Instance
   192→	// stop if not nil is the per-registry stop chan. If null, the server stop chan should be used to Run the registry.
   193→	stop <-chan struct{}
   194→}
   195→
   196→type Options struct {
   197→	MeshHolder      mesh.Holder
   198→	ConfigClusterID cluster.ID
   199→}

   201→// NewController 
... (truncated)
35-assistanttool_useRead
36-usertool_resultRead
   550→		reason.Merge(pr.Reason)
   551→		reason.Merge(other.Reason)
   552→	}
   553→	merged := &PushRequest{
   554→		// Keep the first (older) start time
   555→		Start: pr.Start,
   556→
   557→		// If either is full we need a full push
   558→		Full: pr.Full || other.Full,
   559→
   560→		// If either is forced we need a forced push
   561→		Forced: pr.Forced || other.Forced,
   562→
   563→		// The other push context is presumed to be later and more up to date
   564→		Push: other.Push,
   565→
   566→		// Merge the two reasons. Note that we shouldn't deduplicate here, or we would under count
   567→		Reason: reason,
   568→	}
   569→
   570→	if pr.ConfigsUpdated == nil && other.ConfigsUpdated == nil {
   571→		merged.ConfigsUpdated = nil
   572→	} else {
   573→		merged.ConfigsUpdated = make(sets.Set[ConfigKey], len(pr.ConfigsUpdated)+len(other.ConfigsUpdated))
   574→		merged.ConfigsUpdated.Merge(pr.ConfigsUpdated)
   575→		merged.ConfigsUpdated.Merge(other.ConfigsUpdated)
   576→	}
   577→
   578→	if len(pr.AddressesUpdated) > 0 || len(other.AddressesUpdated) > 0 {
   579→		merged.AddressesUpdated = make(sets.Set[string], len(pr.AddressesUpdated)+len(other.AddressesUpdated))
   580→		merged.AddressesUpdated.Merge(pr.AddressesUpdated)
   581→		merged.AddressesUpdated.Merge(other.AddressesUpdated)
   582→	}
   583→
   584→	return merged
   585→}
   586→
   587→func (pr *PushRequest) IsRequest() bool {
   588→	return len(pr.Reason) == 1 && pr.Reason.Has(ProxyRequest)
   589→}
   590→
   591→func (pr *PushRequest) IsProxyUpdate() bool {
   592→	return pr.Reason.Has(ProxyUpdate)
   593→}
   594→
   595→func (pr *PushRequest) PushReason() string {
   596→	if pr.IsRequest() {
   597→		return " request"
   598→	}
   599→	return ""
   600→}

    30→// SvcUpdate is a callback from service discovery when service info changes.
    31→func (s *DiscoveryServer) SvcUpdate(shard model.ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, event model.Event) {
    32→	// When a service deleted, we should cleanup the endpoint shards and also remove keys from EndpointIndex to
    33→	// prevent memory leaks.
    34→	if event == model.EventDelete {
    35→		inboundServiceDeletes.Increment()
    36→		s.Env.EndpointIndex.DeleteServiceShard(shard, hostname, namespace, false)
    37→	} else {
    38→		inboundServiceUpdates.Increment()
    39→	}
    40→}

   105→func edsNeedsPush(req *model.PushRequest, proxy *model.Proxy) bool {
   106→	if res, ok := xdsNeedsPush(req, proxy); ok {
   107→		return res
   108→	}
   109→	for config := range req.ConfigsUpdated {
   110→		if !skippedEdsConfigs.Contains(config.Kind) {
   111→			return true
   112→		}
   113→	}
   114→	return false
   115→}
   116→
   117→func (eds *EdsGenerator) Generate(proxy *model.Proxy, w *model.WatchedResource, req *model.PushRequest) (model.Resources, model.XdsLogDetails, error) {
   118→	if !edsNeedsPush(req, proxy) {
   119→		return nil, model.DefaultXdsLogDetails, nil
   120→	}
   121→	resources, logDetails := eds.buildEndpoints(proxy, req, w)
   122→	return resources, logDetails, nil
   123→}
   124→
   125→func (eds *EdsGenerator) GenerateDeltas(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest,
   126→	w *model.WatchedResource,
   127→) (model.Resources, model.DeletedResources, model.XdsLogDetails, bool, error) {
   128→	if !edsNeedsPush(req, proxy) {
   129→		return nil, nil, model.DefaultXdsLogDetails, false, nil
   130→	}
   131→	if !shouldUseDeltaEds(req) {
   132→		resources, logDetails := eds.buildEndpoints(proxy, req, w)
   133→		return resources, nil, logDetails, false, nil
   134→	}
   135→
   136→	resources, removed, logs := eds.buildDeltaEndpoints(proxy, req, w)
   137→	return resources, removed, logs, true, nil
   138→}
   139→
   140→func shouldUseDeltaEds(req *model.PushRequest) bool {
   141→	if !req.Full {
   142→		return false
   143→	}
   144→	return canSendPartialFullPushes(req)
   145→}
   146→

   148→// This allows us to perform m

    23→type PushQueue struct {
    24→	cond *sync.Cond
    25→
    26→	// pending stores all connections in the queue. If the same connection is enqueued again,
    27→	// the PushRequest will be merged.
    28→	pending map[*Connection]*model.PushRequest
    29→
    30→	// queue maintains ordering of the queue
    31→	queue []*Connection
    32→
    33→	// processing stores all connections that have been Dequeue(), but not MarkDone().
    34→	// The value stored will be initially be nil, but may be populated if the connection is Enqueue().
    35→	// If model.PushRequest is not nil, it will be Enqueued again once MarkDone has been called.
    36→	processing map[*Connection]*model.PushRequest
    37→
    38→	shuttingDown bool
    39→}
    40→

   866→func (ps *PushContext) ExtraWaypointServices(proxy *Proxy, patches *MergedEnvoyFilterWrapper) (sets.Set[NamespacedHostname], sets.String) {
   867→	return ps.extraServicesForProxy(proxy, patches)
   868→}
   869→
   870→// GatewayServices returns the set of services which are referred from the proxy gateways.
   871→func (ps *PushContext) GatewayServices(proxy *Proxy, patches *MergedEnvoyFilterWrapper) []*Service {
   872→	svcs := proxy.SidecarScope.services
   873→
   874→	// host set.
   875→	namespacedHostsFromGateways, hostsFromGateways := ps.extraServicesForProxy(proxy, patches)
   876→	// MergedGateway will be nil when there are no configs in the
   877→	// system during initial installation.
   878→	if proxy.MergedGateway != nil {
   879→		for _, gw := range proxy.MergedGateway.GatewayNameForServer {
   880→			hostsFromGateways.Merge(ps.virtualServiceIndex.destinationsByGateway[gw])
   881→		}
   882→	}
   883→	log.Debugf("GatewayServices: gateway %v is exposing these hosts:%v", proxy.ID, hostsFromGateways)
   884→
   885→	gwSvcs := make([]*Service, 0, len(svcs))
   886→
   887→	for _, s := range svcs {
   888→		svcHost := string(s.Hostname)
   889→		if hostsFromGateways.Contains(svcHost) || namespacedHostsFromGateways.Contains(NamespacedHostname{
   890→			Hostname:  s.Hostname,
   891→			Namespace: s.Attributes.Namespace,
   892→		}) {
   893→			gwSvcs = append(gwSvcs, s)
   894→		}
   895→	}
   896→
   897→	log.Debugf("GatewayServices: gateways len(services)=%d, len(filtered)=%d", len(svcs), len(gwSvcs))
   898→
   899→	return gwSvcs
   900→}

  1076→	return nil

  1342→// InitContext will initialize the data structures used for code generation.
  1343→// This should be called before starting the push, from the thread creating
  1344→// the push context.
  1345→func (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest) {
  1346→	// Acquire a lock to ensure we don't concurrently initialize the same PushContext.
  1347→	// If this does happen, one thread will block then exit early from InitDone=true
  1348→	ps.initializeMutex.Lock()
  1349→	defer ps.initializeMutex.Unlock()
  1350→	if ps.InitDone.Load() {
  1351→		return
  1352→	}
  1353→
  1354→	ps.Mesh = env.Mesh()
  1355→	ps.Networks = env.MeshNetworks()
  1356→
  1357→	// Must be initialized first as initServiceRegistry/VirtualServices/Destrules
  1358→	// use the default export map.
  1359→	ps.initDefaultExportMaps()
  1360→
  1361→	// create new or incremental update
  1362→	if pushReq == nil || oldPushContext == nil || !oldPushContext.InitDone.Load() || pushReq.Forced {
  1363→		ps.createNewContext(env)
  1364→	} else {
  1365→		ps.updateContext(env, oldPushContext, pushReq)
  1366→	}
  1367→
  1368→	ps.networkMgr = env.NetworkManager
  1369→
  1370→	ps.clusterLocalHosts = env.ClusterLocal().GetClusterLocalHosts()
  1371→
  1372→	ps.InitDone.Store(true)
  1373→}
  1374→

The architecture document has been written to `/workspace/documentation.md`. Here is a summary of what it covers:

**1. DiscoveryServer** — Explains the gRPC server structure, how it supports both SotW and Delta xDS v3, the debouncing pipeline (`pushChannel` → `debounce()` → `Push()`), the concurrent push semaphore (`concurrentPushLimit`), and the LRU cache with dependency-keyed eviction.

**2. ADS and the Connection Model** — Covers `Stream()` establishment (rate limiting, auth, readiness guard), the `Connection` struct (proxy metadata, watched resources, push channel), `processRequest()` (nonce/ACK suppression, per-type push), `pushConnection()` (SidecarScope recomputation, ordered push dispatch), and `StartPush()` (queue-with-merge broadcast).

**3. PushContext** — Documents all pre-indexed sub-structures (`serviceIndex`, `virtualServiceIndex`, `destinationRuleIndex`, `sidecarIndex`), the full vs. incremental `InitContext()` path (only rebuilding what changed), the translation pipeline (VirtualService → RouteConfiguration, DestinationRule → Cluster, DestinationRule priority rules), and metrics/error tracking via `ProxyStatus`.

**4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster** — Describes the `serviceregistry.Instance` interface, the Kubernetes controller's informer-based watchers (Services, EndpointSlices, Pods, Nodes), the aggregate controller's multi-registry fan-out, how remote clusters are added at runtime via `multicluster.Controller`, and the critical EDS vs. full-push distinction (pod churn = incremental EDS; new/deleted service = full CDS push).

Here's a summary of what the document covers:

---

**Document Structure** (`/workspace/documentation.md`):

**1. DiscoveryServer** (`pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`)
- The gRPC server struct with key fields: `adsClients`, `pushChannel`, `pushQueue`, `concurrentPushLimit`, `Cache`, `Generators`
- Both SotW and Delta xDS v3 protocol support
- The debounce pipeline: events arrive via `ConfigUpdate()` → `pushChannel` → `debounce()` (100ms quiet / 10s max) → `Push()` → `initPushContext()` → `AdsPushAll()`
- Concurrent push limiting via a semaphore channel (`features.PushThrottle`, default 100)
- LRU cache with dependency-tracked eviction (`dropCacheForRequest`)
- Full server lifecycle: `NewDiscoveryServer` → `CachesSynced` (readiness gate) → `Start` goroutines → `Shutdown`

**2. ADS Connection Model** (`pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`)
- `Stream()` entry point: rate limiting, mTLS authentication, server readiness check
- The `Connection` type: wraps gRPC stream + `model.Proxy` (with SidecarScope, WatchedResources, push channel)
- `initConnection`: registers proxy in `adsClients` before initialization completes to avoid missing pushes
- `processRequest`: ACK suppression via nonce, per-type push dispatch
- `pushConnection`: recomputes proxy state, checks `ProxyNeedsPush`, pushes in CDS→EDS→LDS→RDS order
- `PushQueue` with merge-on-enqueue: fast-moving config won't grow the queue for slow proxies

**3. PushContext** (`pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`)
- Pre-indexed snapshot: `serviceIndex`, `virtualServiceIndex`, `destinationRuleIndex`, `sidecarIndex`, `gatewayIndex`, `envoyFiltersByNam
... (truncated)

If updates are debounce they will be merged.\n\tvar req *model.PushRequest\n\n\tfree := true\n\tfreeCh := make(chan struct{}, 1)\n\n\tpush := func(req *model.PushRequest, debouncedEvents int, startDebounce time.Time) {\n\t\tpushFn(req)\n\t\tupdateSent.Add(int64(debouncedEvents))\n\t\tdebounceTime.Record(time.Since(startDebounce).Seconds())\n\t\tfreeCh <- struct{}{}\n\t}\n\n\tpushWorker := func() {\n\t\teventDelay := time.Since(startDebounce)\n\t\tquietTime := time.Since(lastConfigUpdateTime)\n\t\t// it has been too long or quiet enough\n\t\tif eventDelay >= opts.debounceMax || quietTime >= opts.DebounceAfter {\n\t\t\tif req != nil {\n\t\t\t\tpushCounter++\n\t\t\t\tif req.ConfigsUpdated == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Push debounce stable[%d] %d for reason %s: %v since last change, %v since last push, full=%v\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\tpushCounter, debouncedEvents, reasonsUpdated(req),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tquietTime, eventDelay, req.Full)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Push debounce stable[%d] %d for config %s: %v since last change, %v since last push, full=%v\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\tpushCounter, debouncedEvents, configsUpdated(req),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tquietTime, eventDelay, req.Full)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tfree = false\n\t\t\t\tgo push(req, debouncedEvents, startDebounce)\n\t\t\t\treq = nil\n\t\t\t\tdebouncedEvents = 0\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\ttimeChan = time.After(opts.DebounceAfter - quietTime)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-freeCh:\n\t\t\tfree = true\n\t\t\tpushWorker()\n\t\tcase r := <-ch:\n\t\t\t// If reason is not set, record it as an unknown reason\n\t\t\tif len(r.Reason) == 0 {\n\t\t\t\tr.Reason = model.NewReasonStats(model.UnknownTrigger)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif !opts.enableEDSDebounce && !r.Full {\n\t\t\t\t// trigger push now, just for EDS\n\t\t\t\tgo func(req *model.PushRequest) {\n\t\t\t\t\tpushFn(req)\n\t\t\t\t\tupdateSent.Inc()\n\t\t\t\t}(r)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tlastConfigUpdateTime = time.Now()\n\t\t\tif debouncedEvents == 0 {\n\t\t\t\ttimeChan = time.After(opts.DebounceAfter)\n\t\t\t\tstartDebounce = lastConfigUpdateTime\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdebouncedEvents++\n\n\t\t\treq = req.Merge(r)\n\t\tcase <-timeChan:\n\t\t\tif free {\n\t\t\t\tpushWorker()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc configsUpdated(req *model.PushRequest) string {\n\tconfigs := \"\"\n\tfor key := range req.ConfigsUpdated {\n\t\tconfigs += key.String()\n\t\tbreak\n\t}\n\tif len(req.ConfigsUpdated) > 1 {\n\t\tmore := \" and \" + strconv.Itoa(len(req.ConfigsUpdated)-1) + \" more configs\"\n\t\tconfigs += more\n\t}\n\treturn configs\n}\n\nfunc reasonsUpdated(req *model.PushRequest) string {\n\tvar (\n\t\treason0, reason1            model.TriggerReason\n\t\treason0Cnt, reason1Cnt, idx int\n\t)\n\tfor r, cnt := range req.Reason {\n\t\tif idx == 0 {\n\t\t\treason0, reason0Cnt = r, cnt\n\t\t} else if idx == 1 {\n\t\t\treason1, reason1Cnt = r, cnt\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tidx++\n\t}\n\n\tswitch len(req.Reason) {\n\tcase 0:\n\t\treturn \"unknown\"\n\tcase 1:\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d\", reason0, reason0Cnt)\n\tcase 2:\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d and %s:%d\", reason0, reason0Cnt, reason1, reason1Cnt)\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d and %d(%d) more reasons\", reason0, reason0Cnt, Client will connect to another\n\t// instance in best case, or retry with backoff.\n\twait, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, time.Second)\n\tdefer cancel()\n\treturn s.RequestRateLimit.Wait(wait)\n}\n\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) NextVersion() string {\n\treturn time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339) + \"/\" + strconv.FormatUint(s.pushVersion.Inc(), 10)\n}\n",

If it is already pending, pushInfo will be merged.\n// ServiceEntry updates will be added together, and full will be set if either were full\nfunc (p *PushQueue) Enqueue(con *Connection, pushRequest *model.PushRequest) {\n\tp.cond.L.Lock()\n\tdefer p.cond.L.Unlock()\n\n\tif p.shuttingDown {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// If its already in progress, merge the info and return\n\tif request, f := p.processing[con]; f {\n\t\tp.processing[con] = request.CopyMerge(pushRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif request, f := p.pending[con]; f {\n\t\tp.pending[con] = request.CopyMerge(pushRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tp.pending[con] = pushRequest\n\tp.queue = append(p.queue, con)\n\t// Signal waiters on Dequeue that a new item is available\n\tp.cond.Signal()\n}\n\n// Remove a proxy from the queue. Input
{
  "content": "# Istio Pilot Discovery Service: Architecture Document\n\n## Overview\n\nIstio Pilot's discovery service is the control plane component responsible for translating Istio's high-level configuration (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, ServiceEntries, Gateways, Sidecars) and Kubernetes service registry state into Envoy-native xDS resources, then streaming those resources to all connected proxies over persistent gRPC connections. The subsystem is implemented in `pilot/pkg/xds/` and `pilot/pkg/model/`, with config translation in `pilot/pkg/networking/core/`.\n\nThe four interconnected components are:\n\n1. **DiscoveryServer** \u2014 the gRPC server and push orchestrator\n2. **ADS Connection Model** \u2014 per-proxy stream lifecycle and push dispatch\n3. **PushContext** \u2014 the immutable configuration snapshot and translation layer\n4. **Service Registry** \u2014 the service/endpoint discovery layer, including multi-cluster support\n\n---\n\n## 1. DiscoveryServer \u2014 The xDS gRPC Server\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\n### Struct Definition\n\n`DiscoveryServer` is the central object. Its key fields reveal the design:\n\n```go\ntype DiscoveryServer struct {\n    Env                 *model.Environment       // access to all Istio config stores\n    Generators          map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator  // pluggable resource generators\n    ProxyNeedsPush      func(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) (*model.PushRequest, bool)\n    concurrentPushLimit chan struct{}             // semaphore bounding parallel pushes\n    RequestRateLimit    *rate.Limiter            // per-connection rate limiter\n    pushChannel         chan *model.PushRequest   // unbuffered input to debouncer\n    pushQueue           *PushQueue               // per-proxy ordered push work queue\n    adsClients          map[string]*Connection   // all connected proxies, keyed by connection ID\n    adsClientsMutex     sync.RWMutex\n    Cache               model.XdsCache           // LRU cache for generated xDS resources\n    DebounceOptions     DebounceOptions\n}\n```\n\n### xDS Protocol Support\n\n`DiscoveryServer` registers itself with the gRPC server via `Register`, which calls `discovery.RegisterAggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer`. This means it implements both:\n\n- **State-of-the-World (SotW) ADS**: `StreamAggregatedResources` \u2192 `Stream()` in `ads.go`\n- **Incremental (Delta) ADS**: `DeltaAggregatedResources` \u2192 `StreamDeltas()` in `delta.go`\n\nBoth modes share the same underlying push path and the same `PushContext`. The difference is in how resource changes are communicated: SotW sends the complete set of resources for a type on every push, while Delta sends only the added/modified and removed resources. Delta mode uses `GenerateDeltas()` on generators (e.g., `EdsGenerator.GenerateDeltas`) which can return both added and removed resources.\n\n### Push Type Classification\n\nThe xDS push type matrix is determined per resource type:\n\n| Resource Type | Triggered by | Full vs. Incremental |\n|---|---|---|\n| CDS (Clusters) | DestinationRule, ServiceEntry, VirtualService (for gateways) | Full push (rebuilds PushContext) |\n| LDS (Listeners) | VirtualService, Sidecar, AuthorizationPolicy, etc. | Full push |\n| RDS (Routes) | VirtualService changes | Full push |\n| EDS (Endpoints) | Pod/Endpoint changes | Incremental push (no PushContext rebuild) |\n\nThe push type is determined by `PushRequest.Full`: `true` means a full push (PushContext is rebuilt, all generators run), `false` means incremental (PushContext reused, only EDS generators run).\n\n### Debouncing\n\nConfig changes arrive via `ConfigUpdate(req *model.PushRequest)`, which writes to `pushChannel`. The `handleUpdates` goroutine runs `debounce()`:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:327\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) handleUpdates(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n    debounce(s.pushChannel, stopCh, s.DebounceOptions, s.Push, s.CommittedUpdates)\n}\n```\n\nThe debounce function merges incoming `PushRequest` values \u2014 if two config changes arrive quickly, their `ConfigsUpdated` sets are unioned and the `Full` flag is OR'd. The debouncer waits `DebounceAfter` (default 100ms) since the last event, or triggers immediately if `debounceMax` (default 10s) has elapsed without relief. EDS pushes bypass debounce entirely (they go directly to `Push()`) unless `enableEDSDebounce` is set.\n\nWhen the debounce timer fires, `Push()` is called:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:258\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Push(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    if !req.Full {\n        req.Push = s.globalPushContext()\n        s.dropCacheForRequest(req)\n        s.AdsPushAll(req)\n        return\n    }\n    // For full push: rebuild PushContext, then broadcast\n    push := s.initPushContext(req, oldPushContext, versionLocal)\n    req.Push = push\n    s.AdsPushAll(req)\n}\n```\n\n### Concurrent Push Limiting\n\nAfter `AdsPushAll` enqueues all connections in the `PushQueue`, the `sendPushes` goroutine dequeues connections and dispatches them:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:457\nfunc doSendPushes(stopCh <-chan struct{}, semaphore chan struct{}, queue *PushQueue) {\n    for {\n        semaphore <- struct{}{}  // blocks when concurrentPushLimit connections are in flight\n        client, push, shuttingdown := queue.Dequeue()\n        go func() {\n            pushEv := &Event{pushRequest: push, done: doneFunc}\n            select {\n            case client.PushCh() <- pushEv:  // delivers to connection's push goroutine\n            case <-closed:\n                doneFunc()\n            }\n        }()\n    }\n}\n```\n\n`concurrentPushLimit` defaults to `features.PushThrottle` (default 100). This prevents the server from overwhelming proxies or its own CPU when the fleet is large.\n\n### Cache Management\n\n`DiscoveryServer.Cache` is a `model.XdsCache` (implemented by `typedXdsCache` in `pilot/pkg/model/typed_xds_cache.go`). Generators (EDS, CDS, RDS) store computed Envoy resources in this cache keyed by a request-specific cache key. On the next push, they first check the cache before recomputing.\n\nCache invalidation is driven by `dropCacheForRequest`:\n\n- **Forced push** (`req.Forced = true`): `ClearAll()` \u2014 invalidates everything\n- **Scoped push**: `Clear(req.ConfigsUpdated)` \u2014 only entries whose declared dependencies include any of the changed config keys are evicted\n\nEach cached entry declares its dependent configs via `DependentConfigs() []ConfigHash`. The LRU cache tracks this reverse mapping to enable targeted eviction.\n\n### Lifecycle\n\n```\nNewDiscoveryServer()\n    \u2192 initJwksResolver()\n\nStart(stopCh)\n    \u2192 go WorkloadEntryController.Run()\n    \u2192 go handleUpdates()    // debounce goroutine\n    \u2192 go periodicRefreshMetrics()\n    \u2192 go sendPushes()       // push dispatch goroutine\n    \u2192 go Cache.Run()        // cache background work\n\nRegister(grpcServer)\n    \u2192 RegisterAggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer()\n\nCachesSynced()             // called when all informers have synced; enables new connections\n\nShutdown()\n    \u2192 closeJwksResolver()\n    \u2192 pushQueue.ShutDown()\n```\n\nThe server refuses new connections until `CachesSynced()` is called. This ensures proxies do not connect to an empty-cache server and lose their existing configuration (see `ads.go:Stream()` \u2014 it returns `codes.Unavailable` if `!s.IsServerReady()`).\n\n---\n\n## 2. ADS and the Connection Model\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`, `pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go`, `pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen.go`\n\n### Stream Establishment\n\nWhen Envoy connects and opens an ADS stream, `StreamAggregatedResources` is invoked, which calls `Stream()`:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:188\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n    if !s.IsServerReady() {\n        return status.Error(codes.Unavailable, \"server is not ready\")\n    }\n    // Rate limit new connections\n    if err := s.WaitForRequestLimit(stream.Context()); err != nil {\n        return status.Errorf(codes.ResourceExhausted, ...)\n    }\n    // Authenticate (mTLS SPIFFE identity or JWT)\n    ids, err := s.authenticate(ctx)\n    // Ensure push context exists\n    s.globalPushContext().InitContext(s.Env, nil, nil)\n    // Create connection wrapper\n    con := newConnection(peerAddr, stream)\n    con.ids = ids\n    con.s = s\n    return xds.Stream(con)  // enters the read/push loop in pkg/xds\n}\n```\n\nThe connection is then handed to the generic `xds.Stream()` loop (in `pkg/xds/`), which calls back into Pilot's `Connection` methods for each event.\n\n### The Connection Type\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:71\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection                    // base: stream, pushCh, initialized state\n    node        *core.Node            // raw Envoy node proto (for efficient re-serialization)\n    proxy       *model.Proxy          // parsed, enriched proxy metadata\n    deltaStream DeltaDiscoveryStream  // set if using Delta xDS, nil for SotW\n    deltaReqChan chan *discovery.DeltaDiscoveryRequest\n    s           *DiscoveryServer\n    ids         []string              // SPIFFE identities from mTLS certificate\n}\n```\n\n`Connection` wraps the raw gRPC stream with Pilot-specific state. The `proxy` field holds:\n- IP addresses, cluster ID, namespace, service account\n- Proxy type (`SidecarProxy`, `Router` for gateways, `Waypoint`, `Ztunnel`)\n- Computed `SidecarScope` (which services/routes are visible to this proxy)\n- `WatchedResources` map: per-type subscription state (resource names, nonce, version)\n- `LastPushContext` and `LastPushTime` for cache correctness\n\n### Connection Initialization\n\nThe first `DiscoveryRequest` from Envoy carries the `Node` proto with metadata. `initConnection` processes it:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:240\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) initConnection(node *core.Node, con *Connection, ids []string) error {\n    proxy, err := s.initProxyMetadata(node)  // parse metadata, node ID\n    // resolve cluster aliases\n    proxy.LastPushContext = s.globalPushContext()\n    con.SetID(connectionID(proxy.ID))\n    con.proxy = proxy\n    s.authorize(con, ids)              // check RBAC: is this identity allowed to connect?\n    s.addCon(con.ID(), con)            // register in adsClients map\n    defer con.MarkInitialized()        // unblock any pending pushes for this con\n    s.initializeProxy(con)             // compute SidecarScope, service targets, labels\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\nNote the ordering: `addCon` registers before `initializeProxy` completes. This prevents a race where a new push context is created between registration and initialization \u2014 the proxy will receive the push even if it hasn't finished initializing (which is safe because `MarkInitialized` gates the push delivery).\n\n### Request Processing\n\nEach `DiscoveryRequest` from Envoy is dispatched to `processRequest`:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:139\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) processRequest(req *discovery.DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection) error {\n    // Health check type is handled specially (WorkloadEntry health)\n    if req.TypeUrl == v3.HealthInfoType { ... }\n    // Debug requests get an immediate forced response\n    if strings.HasPrefix(req.TypeUrl, v3.DebugType) { ... }\n\n    // ShouldRespond checks nonce/version to suppress ACK loops\n    shouldRespond, delta := xds.ShouldRespond(con.proxy, con.ID(), req)\n    if !shouldRespond { return nil }\n\n    request := &model.PushRequest{\n        Full:   true,\n        Push:   con.proxy.LastPushContext,\n        Reason: model.NewReasonStats(model.ProxyRequest),\n        Start:  con.proxy.LastPushTime,\n        Delta:  delta,\n        Forced: true,\n    }\n    return s.pushXds(con, con.proxy.GetWatchedResource(req.TypeUrl), request)\n}\n```\n\nThe `ShouldRespond` logic prevents re-sending resources that the proxy already acknowledged. When Envoy sends a request for a type it already has (with a matching nonce), it's treated as an ACK and suppressed.\n\n### Push Dispatch\n\n`pushConnection` is called when the push goroutine receives an `Event`:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:472\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) pushConnection(con *Connection, pushEv *Event) error {\n    pushRequest := pushEv.pushRequest\n    if pushRequest.Full {\n        s.computeProxyState(con.proxy, pushRequest)  // recompute SidecarScope etc.\n    }\n    pushRequest, needsPush := s.ProxyNeedsPush(con.proxy, pushRequest)\n    if !needsPush { return nil }\n\n    // Push each watched resource type in order: CDS, EDS, LDS, RDS, ...\n    wrl := con.watchedResourcesByOrder()\n    for _, w := range wrl {\n        if err := s.pushXds(con, w, pushRequest); err != nil {\n            return err\n        }\n    }\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\nThe push order \u2014 CDS \u2192 EDS \u2192 LDS \u2192 RDS \u2014 is important: Envoy processes CDS first (to learn cluster definitions), then EDS (endpoints for those clusters), then LDS (listeners that reference clusters), then RDS (route configs referenced by listeners). Sending in the wrong order would cause Envoy to reference unknown resources.\n\n### `pushXds` \u2014 The Generator Dispatch\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen.go:101\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) pushXds(con *Connection, w *model.WatchedResource, req *model.PushRequest) error {\n    gen := s.findGenerator(w.TypeUrl, con)  // lookup: proxy-type/typeURL or just typeURL\n    res, logdata, err := gen.Generate(con.proxy, w, req)\n    if err != nil || res == nil { return err }\n\n    resp := &discovery.DiscoveryResponse{\n        TypeUrl:     w.TypeUrl,\n        VersionInfo: req.Push.PushVersion,\n        Nonce:       nonce(req.Push.PushVersion),\n        Resources:   xds.ResourcesToAny(res),\n    }\n    return xds.Send(con, resp)\n}\n```\n\n### The `StartPush` Broadcast\n\n`StartPush` iterates over all registered connections and enqueues each for a push:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:582\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) StartPush(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    req.Start = time.Now()\n    for _, p := range s.AllClients() {\n        s.pushQueue.Enqueue(p, req)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n`PushQueue` (`pilot/pkg/xds/pushqueue.go`) is an ordered work queue with merge semantics: if a connection is already pending in the queue, a new enqueue merges the `PushRequest` (OR-ing the `Full` flag, unioning `ConfigsUpdated`). This prevents queue growth when fast-moving config triggers multiple pushes before the first one is dispatched to a slow proxy.\n\n---\n\n## 3. PushContext \u2014 Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`, `pilot/pkg/networking/core/`\n\n### What PushContext Holds\n\n`PushContext` is an immutable (after initialization) snapshot of all Istio configuration, pre-indexed for efficient per-proxy lookup:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go:207\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Services indexed by exportTo visibility, hostname, namespace\n    ServiceIndex        serviceIndex\n    // VirtualServices indexed by gateway and namespace\n    virtualServiceIndex virtualServiceIndex\n    // DestinationRules indexed by namespace with specificity ordering\n    destinationRuleIndex destinationRuleIndex\n    // Sidecar resources, with lazy-computed defaults per namespace\n    sidecarIndex        sidecarIndex\n    // Gateway resources by namespace\n    gatewayIndex        gatewayIndex\n    // EnvoyFilter patches by namespace\n    envoyFiltersByNamespace map[string][]*EnvoyFilterWrapper\n    // WasmPlugin extensions by namespace\n    wasmPluginsByNamespace  map[string][]*WasmPluginWrapper\n    // Authentication policies (PeerAuthentication, RequestAuthentication)\n    AuthnPolicies       *AuthenticationPolicies\n    // Authorization policies (AuthorizationPolicy)\n    AuthzPolicies       *AuthorizationPolicies\n    // Telemetry resources\n    Telemetry           *Telemetries\n    // Proxy-level config (ProxyConfig)\n    ProxyConfigs        *ProxyConfigs\n    // Mesh-wide config\n    Mesh                *meshconfig.MeshConfig\n    // Metrics/error tracking across this push cycle\n    ProxyStatus         map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n    // Push version string (used as xDS VersionInfo)\n    PushVersion         string\n}\n```\n\nThe `serviceIndex` pre-computes visibility-based views: `public` (exportTo `*`), `privateByNamespace` (exportTo `.`), `exportedToNamespace` (specific namespace targets). This means per-proxy service list lookups are O(1) hash maps instead of O(N\u00d7M) filter loops.\n\nSimilarly, `virtualServiceIndex` maintains `publicByGateway`, `privateByNamespaceAndGateway`, and `exportedToNamespaceByGateway` maps, enabling efficient lookup of which VirtualServices apply to a given gateway or sidecar scope.\n\n`destinationRuleIndex` consolidates multiple DestinationRules that match the same host (via wildcard or specific hostname) into a `ConsolidatedDestRule`, merging their subsets and traffic policies according to the selection priority rules.\n\n### InitContext \u2014 Rebuilding the Snapshot\n\n`InitContext` is called by `DiscoveryServer.initPushContext` at the start of each full push. It takes an optional `oldPushContext` to enable incremental rebuilding:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go:1345\nfunc (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest) {\n    ps.initializeMutex.Lock()   // guard against concurrent init\n    defer ps.initializeMutex.Unlock()\n    if ps.InitDone.Load() { return }  // idempotent\n\n    ps.Mesh = env.Mesh()\n    ps.Networks = env.MeshNetworks()\n    ps.initDefaultExportMaps()\n\n    if pushReq == nil || oldPushContext == nil || !oldPushContext.InitDone.Load() || pushReq.Forced {\n        ps.createNewContext(env)   // full rebuild\n    } else {\n        ps.updateContext(env, oldPushContext, pushReq)  // incremental\n    }\n    ps.InitDone.Store(true)\n}\n```\n\n**Full rebuild** (`createNewContext`) calls:\n1. `initServiceRegistry` \u2014 fetches all services from `env.Services()` (the aggregate registry), builds `ServiceIndex`\n2. `initKubernetesGateways` \u2014 processes Gateway API resources\n3. `initVirtualServices` \u2014 loads all VirtualServices and builds the namespace/gateway indexes\n4. `initDestinationRules` \u2014 loads and consolidates all DestinationRules\n5. `initAuthnPolicies`, `initAuthorizationPolicies` \u2014 security policy indexes\n6. `initTelemetry`, `initProxyConfigs`, `initWasmPlugins`, `initEnvoyFilters`\n7. `initGateways` \u2014 indexes Istio Gateway resources\n8. `initSidecarScopes` \u2014 converts `Sidecar` resources into `SidecarScope` objects per namespace\n\n**Incremental rebuild** (`updateContext`) inspects `pushReq.ConfigsUpdated` to determine which sub-indexes need rebuilding:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go:1397\nfunc (ps *PushContext) updateContext(env, oldPushContext, pushReq) {\n    for conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated {\n        switch conf.Kind {\n        case kind.ServiceEntry, kind.DNSName:\n            servicesChanged = true\n        case kind.DestinationRule:\n            destinationRulesChanged = true\n        case kind.VirtualService:\n            virtualServicesChanged = true\n        case kind.Gateway:\n            gatewayChanged = true\n        case kind.Sidecar:\n            sidecarsChanged = true\n        // ... etc\n        }\n    }\n    // Only rebuild changed sub-indexes; copy the rest from oldPushContext\n    if servicesChanged { ps.initServiceRegistry(...) } else { ps.ServiceIndex = oldPushContext.ServiceIndex }\n    // ... similarly for each sub-index\n    // Sidecar scopes are rebuilt if services, virtual services, destination rules, OR sidecars changed\n    if servicesChanged || virtualServicesChanged || destinationRulesChanged || sidecarsChanged {\n        ps.initSidecarScopes(env)\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis optimization avoids scanning all VirtualServices if only a DestinationRule changed, for example.\n\n### Config Translation: VirtualService \u2192 RouteConfiguration\n\nThe translation from Istio resources to Envoy resources happens in `pilot/pkg/networking/core/`. The key interface is:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/networking/core/configgen.go:28\ntype ConfigGenerator interface {\n    BuildListeners(node *model.Proxy, push *model.PushContext) []*listener.Listener\n    BuildClusters(node *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) ([]*discovery.Resource, model.XdsLogDetails)\n    BuildDeltaClusters(proxy *model.Proxy, updates *model.PushRequest, watched *model.WatchedResource) (...)\n    BuildHTTPRoutes(node *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest, routeNames []string) ([]*discovery.Resource, model.XdsLogDetails)\n    BuildNameTable(node *model.Proxy, push *model.PushContext) *dnsProto.NameTable\n    BuildExtensionConfiguration(node *model.Proxy, push *model.PushContext, ...) []*core.TypedExtensionConfig\n}\n```\n\n`ConfigGeneratorImpl` (in `pilot/pkg/networking/core/configgen.go`) implements this interface. Generators in `pilot/pkg/xds/` call into it:\n\n- `LdsGenerator.Generate` \u2192 `configgen.BuildListeners`\n- `CdsGenerator.Generate` / `GenerateDeltas` \u2192 `configgen.BuildClusters` / `BuildDeltaClusters`\n- `RdsGenerator.Generate` \u2192 `configgen.BuildHTTPRoutes`\n- `EdsGenerator.Generate` / `GenerateDeltas` \u2192 endpoint builder in `pilot/pkg/xds/endpoints/`\n\n**VirtualService \u2192 RouteConfiguration:**\n`BuildHTTPRoutes` iterates over VirtualServices applicable to the proxy (from `proxy.SidecarScope` for sidecars, or `PushContext.VirtualServicesForGateway` for gateways). For each VirtualService, it produces an Envoy `RouteConfiguration` containing `VirtualHost` entries. HTTP match conditions (`headers`, `uri`, `method`), retries, timeouts, fault injection, and traffic mirroring defined in the VirtualService spec are translated directly into Envoy's `route.Route` proto. Destination host+subset references become Envoy cluster names in the form `outbound|<port>|<subset>|<hostname>`.\n\n**DestinationRule \u2192 Cluster:**\n`BuildClusters` calls the cluster builder (`pilot/pkg/networking/core/cluster_builder.go`) for each service visible to the proxy. The cluster builder:\n1. Creates an Envoy `Cluster` for each service port (named `outbound|<port>||<hostname>`)\n2. Looks up the applicable `DestinationRule` via `PushContext.destinationRule(proxyNamespace, service)`, which applies the specificity and namespace priority rules\n3. Translates `TrafficPolicy` (connection pool settings, circuit breakers, load balancing, TLS mode) into Envoy cluster fields\n4. For each DR subset, creates an additional cluster named `outbound|<port>|<subset>|<hostname>` with the subset's overrides applied\n\n**EnvoyFilter Patching:**\nAfter generating base resources, `envoyfilter` patches (`MERGE_PATCH`, `ADD_TO_ARRAY`, `REPLACE`, `REMOVE`) from `EnvoyFilter` resources are applied to modify or extend the generated Envoy proto messages. This is the primary extension point for custom Envoy configuration.\n\n### DestinationRule Selection Priority\n\nThe `destinationRule()` function (`pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go:1244`) implements a four-level priority:\n1. Namespace-local rules in the proxy's own namespace\n2. Rules in the service's namespace (exported to the proxy's namespace)\n3. Rules in the root (config) namespace\n\nThis allows platform operators to define mesh-wide defaults in `istio-system` while allowing teams to override for their own services.\n\n### Metrics and Error Tracking\n\n`PushContext` implements `Metrics` to collect per-push status:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) AddMetric(metric monitoring.Metric, key string, proxyID, msg string)\n```\n\nGenerators call `AddMetric` to record conditions like:\n- `EndpointNoPod` \u2014 an endpoint IP with no matching pod (usually transient during pod startup)\n- `ProxyStatusNoService` \u2014 a proxy not selected by any Service\n- `DuplicatedSubsets` \u2014 conflicting subset definitions across DestinationRules\n- `ProxyStatusClusterNoInstances` \u2014 a cluster with zero healthy endpoints\n\nAt the end of each push cycle, `UpdateMetrics` flushes these counters to Prometheus. The debug endpoint (`/debug/push-status`) exposes the last push's `ProxyStatus` map as JSON.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/`, `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go`, `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go`, `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go`\n\n### The ServiceRegistry Interface\n\nThe core abstraction is `serviceregistry.Instance`:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/instance.go:25\ntype Instance interface {\n    model.Controller      // Run(stop), AppendServiceHandler, AppendWorkloadHandler, HasSynced\n    model.ServiceDiscovery // Services(), GetService(), InstancesByPort(), GetProxyWorkloadLabels()\n    Provider() provider.ID\n    Cluster() cluster.ID\n}\n```\n\n`model.ServiceDiscovery` is the query interface that `PushContext.initServiceRegistry` uses to enumerate services. `model.Controller` provides the event handler registration points used to trigger xDS pushes.\n\n### The Kubernetes Controller\n\n`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/Controller` is a `serviceregistry.Instance` backed by Kubernetes informers:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go:189\ntype Controller struct {\n    client     kubelib.Client\n    queue      queue.Instance          // work queue for event processing\n    namespaces kclient.Client[*v1.Namespace]\n    services   kclient.Client[*v1.Service]\n    endpoints  *endpointSliceController\n    nodes      kclient.Client[*v1.Node]\n    pods       *PodCache\n    servicesMap map[host.Name]*model.Service  // hostname -> Service\n    // ...\n}\n```\n\nThe controller watches:\n- **Services**: converted to `model.Service` objects with port mappings, labels, and visibility attributes\n- **EndpointSlices** (via `endpointSliceController`): reconciled against Pod state to produce `model.IstioEndpoint` objects carrying IP, port, labels, locality, and health status\n- **Pods** (via `PodCache`): used to enrich endpoints with workload labels (for traffic policy matching) and locality information from the node's `topology.kubernetes.io/region` and `topology.kubernetes.io/zone` labels\n- **Nodes**: used to build node-IP maps for NodePort service translation and multi-network gateway detection\n\nWhen a Service or EndpointSlice event is received, the controller calls back into `XDSUpdater` (the `DiscoveryServer`):\n\n```go\n// endpoint change \u2192 EDSUpdate\ns.XDSUpdater.EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, endpoints)\n\n// service change \u2192 SvcUpdate + ConfigUpdate\ns.XDSUpdater.SvcUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, event)\ns.XDSUpdater.ConfigUpdate(&PushRequest{Full: true, Reason: ServiceUpdate})\n```\n\n### The Aggregate Controller\n\n`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/Controller` fans out queries to all registered registries and merges their results:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go:42\ntype Controller struct {\n    registries        []*registryEntry  // ordered: Kubernetes first, then ServiceEntry\n    configClusterID   cluster.ID\n    handlers          model.ControllerHandlers\n    handlersByCluster map[cluster.ID]*model.ControllerHandlers\n}\n```\n\n`AddRegistryAndRun` adds a new registry (e.g., a newly discovered remote cluster) and starts it. The aggregate controller propagates handler registrations to each registry so that service and network gateway changes in any sub-registry trigger the appropriate `XDSUpdater` callbacks.\n\n`ServiceDiscovery` methods (`Services()`, `GetService()`, `InstancesByPort()`) are implemented by iterating over all registries and merging results, with deduplication where needed (e.g., `AddressInformation` for ambient mode cross-checks registry results).\n\n### Multi-Cluster Support\n\nMulti-cluster is implemented via the `multicluster.Controller` (in `pkg/kube/multicluster/`), which watches the secret-based kubeconfig registry. When a new cluster secret is created, `multicluster.Controller` creates a new `kubecontroller.Controller` for that cluster and calls `aggregate.Controller.AddRegistryAndRun`. Each remote cluster's controller uses its own Kubernetes client but shares the same `XDSUpdater` (the `DiscoveryServer`).\n\nThis means:\n- Services from all clusters are visible in `PushContext.ServiceIndex`\n- Each remote cluster's endpoints are tracked in a separate `ShardKey` within `EndpointIndex`\n- Cluster aliasing (`ClusterAliases` in `DiscoveryServer`) allows a proxy reporting cluster ID `A` to be treated as belonging to cluster ID `B`, enabling cluster renaming scenarios\n\nThe `configClusterID` field in `aggregate.Controller` identifies the primary cluster \u2014 the one from which Istio CRDs (VirtualService, DestinationRule, etc.) are read. For `ServiceEntry`-defined services, the ServiceEntry controller runs only on the config cluster.\n\n### Endpoint Updates and EDS Push Path\n\nWhen a Pod is added, deleted, or changes readiness state, the Kubernetes controller reconciles the EndpointSlice and calls `XDSUpdater.EDSUpdate`:\n\n```go\n// pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go:47\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) EDSUpdate(shard model.ShardKey, serviceName string, namespace string,\n    istioEndpoints []*model.IstioEndpoint,\n) {\n    pushType := s.Env.EndpointIndex.UpdateServiceEndpoints(shard, serviceName, namespace, istioEndpoints, true)\n    if pushType == model.IncrementalPush || pushType == model.FullPush {\n        s.ConfigUpdate(&model.PushRequest{\n            Full:           pushType == model.FullPush,\n            ConfigsUpdated: sets.New(model.ConfigKey{Kind: kind.ServiceEntry, Name: serviceName, Namespace: namespace}),\n            Reason:         model.NewReasonStats(model.EndpointUpdate),\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\n`EndpointIndex.UpdateServiceEndpoints` stores the endpoint shard and returns whether the update requires an incremental or full push:\n- **Incremental EDS push** (`Full: false`): endpoint IPs/ports changed but the service structure did not. Only EDS resources are regenerated; the PushContext is not rebuilt.\n- **Full push** (`Full: true`): returned when a new shard is created (i.e., first endpoints for a service), which can affect cluster discovery (CDS).\n\nThis distinction is central to scalability: most pod churn (rolling deployments, health changes) generates incremental EDS pushes that bypass debouncing and PushContext rebuilding entirely.\n\n`EDSCacheUpdate` is a variant that updates the endpoint shard without triggering a push \u2014 used by batch reconciliation paths that will trigger a single push at the end.\n\n### CDS vs. EDS Trigger Distinction\n\n| Change | Push Type | Reason |\n|---|---|---|\n| Pod added/removed (existing service) | Incremental EDS | Endpoint shard updated; cluster structure unchanged |\n| New service created | Full push (CDS+EDS+LDS) | New cluster must be created in Envoy |\n| Service deleted | Full push | Existing cluster must be removed |\n| DestinationRule changed | Full push (CDS) | Cluster circuit breaker / LB config changes |\n| VirtualService changed | Full push (LDS+RDS) | Listener/route config changes; EDS unaffected |\n| EnvoyFilter changed | Full push (all) | May patch any resource type |\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow: Config Change to xDS Push\n\nThe end-to-end flow from an Istio config change to Envoy receiving updated xDS:\n\n```\n1. User applies a VirtualService CRD change\n        \u2193\n2. Kubernetes informer in config controller fires\n        \u2193\n3. DiscoveryServer.ConfigUpdate() called with PushRequest{Full:true, ConfigsUpdated:{VirtualService/foo}}\n        \u2193\n4. pushChannel receives the PushRequest\n        \u2193\n5. debounce() accumulates events (DebounceAfter=100ms)\n        \u2193\n6. Push(req) called:\n   a. initPushContext() \u2192 NewPushContext() \u2192 InitContext()\n      - updateContext() detects virtualServicesChanged=true\n      - Rebuilds only virtualServiceIndex; copies other indexes from old PushContext\n   b. dropCacheForRequest() \u2192 Cache.Clear({VirtualService/foo}) \u2014 evicts cached RDS entries\n   c. AdsPushAll(req) \u2192 StartPush(req) \u2014 enqueues all connections in PushQueue\n        \u2193\n7. sendPushes() dequeues connections (up to concurrentPushLimit in parallel):\n   For each Connection:\n   a. pushConnection() \u2192 computeProxyState() \u2014 recomputes SidecarScope if needed\n   b. ProxyNeedsPush() \u2014 checks if this proxy is affected by ConfigsUpdated\n      (proxies in unrelated namespaces with Sidecar scoping may be skipped)\n   c. For each WatchedResource in PushOrder:\n      - LdsGenerator.Generate() \u2192 configgen.BuildListeners(proxy, push)\n        \u2192 fetches applicable VirtualServices from virtualServiceIndex\n        \u2192 builds Listener with HCM, route config references\n      - RdsGenerator.Generate() \u2192 configgen.BuildHTTPRoutes(proxy, push, routeNames)\n        \u2192 fetches VirtualServices, translates to Envoy RouteConfigurations\n        \u2192 checks Cache (miss due to eviction in step 6b)\n        \u2192 generates new RouteConfiguration protos\n        \u2192 stores in Cache\n      - CDS and EDS skipped (ldsNeedsPush/cdsNeedsPush returns false for pure VS change)\n   d. DiscoveryResponse sent over gRPC stream\n        \u2193\n8. Envoy receives DiscoveryResponse, applies new listeners and routes\n9. Envoy ACKs with DiscoveryRequest (same nonce) \u2192 ShouldRespond returns false \u2192 ignored\n```\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\n### Custom Resource Generators\n\nThe `Generators` map in `DiscoveryServer` maps type URLs to `model.XdsResourceGenerator` implementations. This is how new xDS resource types are added:\n\n```go\ntype XdsResourceGenerator interface {\n    Generate(proxy *model.Proxy, w *model.WatchedResource, req *model.PushRequest) (Resources, XdsLogDetails, error)\n}\n```\n\nPilot registers built-in generators for CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS, NDS (NameTable), SDS, ECDS (ExtensionConfig), and WorkloadEntry/WorkloadAuthorization types. Custom generators can be registered to handle proprietary type URLs. The `findGenerator` lookup order is:\n1. `proxy.Metadata.Generator + \"/\" + typeURL` (explicit per-connection override)\n2. `proxy.Type + \"/\" + typeURL` (per-proxy-type override, e.g. only for gateways)\n3. `typeURL` (global)\n4. `proxy.XdsResourceGenerator` (connection default, if set in node metadata)\n\nThis allows, for example, a custom generator for MCP (Mesh Configuration Protocol) type URLs to be registered for specific proxy types.\n\n### EnvoyFilter Patching\n\n`EnvoyFilter` resources are the primary extension mechanism for modifying generated Envoy configuration without forking Pilot. They apply `MERGE_PATCH`, `ADD_TO_ARRAY`, `REPLACE`, or `REMOVE` operations to any generated proto at any stage of the listener/cluster/route build. Patches are matched by context (SIDECAR_INBOUND, SIDECAR_OUTBOUND, GATEWAY) and by listener name, cluster name, or route configuration name.\n\nThe patch logic is in `pilot/pkg/networking/core/envoyfilter/`.\n\n### WasmPlugin Extensions\n\n`WasmPlugin` resources allow injecting WebAssembly-based Envoy HTTP or Network filters. These are resolved during `initWasmPlugins` and applied during `BuildListeners` as additional filter entries. The `ECDS` (Extension Config Discovery Service) xDS resource type is used for dynamic Wasm plugin distribution, allowing plugin binaries to be updated without restarting proxies.\n\n### External Service Registries\n\n`serviceregistry.Instance` is an interface. Any service discovery system can implement it (the codebase includes `memory`, `mock`, and `serviceentry` implementations alongside the primary `kube` one). External registries integrate by:\n1. Implementing `model.ServiceDiscovery` for service/endpoint queries\n2. Implementing `model.Controller` for event handler registration\n3. Calling `XDSUpdater.EDSUpdate` / `ConfigUpdate` when their state changes\n4. Registering with `aggregate.Controller.AddRegistryAndRun`\n\n### Telemetry API\n\n`Telemetry` resources are processed by `initTelemetry` and applied during listener construction. They configure per-proxy access logging, tracing, and metrics provider settings without requiring EnvoyFilter patches. The telemetry system is pluggable via the provider model \u2014 `wellknownProviders` in `push_context.go` lists all supported telemetry backends (Zipkin, Datadog, OpenTelemetry, Prometheus, etc.).\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Config Validation Errors\n\nConfig validation happens at admission time via the Istio validation webhook \u2014 by the time a resource reaches `PushContext.InitContext`, it has already passed structural validation. However, semantic errors (referencing a non-existent service, conflicting timeout values) are caught during `initVirtualServices` / `initDestinationRules` and logged as warnings. Invalid configs are typically skipped rather than crashing the push, to minimize blast radius.\n\n### Push Generation Failures\n\n`pushXds` returns any error from `gen.Generate()`. If a generator returns an error (e.g., proto marshal failure), `pushConnection` propagates it, causing the stream to be torn down. Envoy will reconnect and get fresh configuration on the next stream. Generator panics are not currently recovered \u2014 they would crash the goroutine and produce a stream closure. Individual push failures do not block other connections' pushes (each runs in its own goroutine under the semaphore).\n\n### gRPC Send Failures\n\nIf `xds.Send(con, resp)` fails (client disconnected, stream broken), the error propagates from `pushXds` \u2192 `pushConnection` \u2192 the send goroutine, which returns it. The `xds.Stream` read loop (in `pkg/xds/`) detects the error, calls `Connection.Close()` which invokes `closeConnection`, removing the connection from `adsClients`. The `removeCon` function logs an error if the connection ID was not found (which would indicate a bookkeeping bug). After removal, the next `StartPush` will not enqueue this connection.\n\n### Proxy Disconnect Handling\n\n`WorkloadEntryController.OnDisconnect(con)` is called in `closeConnection`. This handles the case of auto-registered `WorkloadEntry` proxies (VM workloads): if a VM's proxy disconnects, its WorkloadEntry health status is updated. For Kubernetes sidecar proxies, disconnect simply removes the connection from `adsClients`.\n\n### Server Not Ready\n\nBefore `CachesSynced()` is called, `Stream()` and `StreamDeltas()` return `codes.Unavailable`. This prevents reconnected Envoys from receiving empty configuration (all services unknown) during Istiod startup. Kubernetes readiness probes check `IsServerReady()` so that the load balancer does not route Envoy connections to Istiod instances still warming up.\n\n### Cache Eviction on Push Failure\n\nIf a push is started but the proxy disconnects mid-push, the `done` callback (`doneFunc` in `doSendPushes`) is called anyway (from the `case <-closed` branch). This calls `queue.MarkDone(client)`, which checks if a new push was queued during the in-flight push (merging it) and re-enqueues if so. This prevents the proxy from being permanently stuck in the `processing` state in `PushQueue`.\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\n| File | Purpose |\n|---|---|\n| `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` | `DiscoveryServer` struct, debounce loop, push orchestration, cache management |\n| `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` | SotW ADS stream handler, `Connection` type, `processRequest`, `pushConnection`, `StartPush`
